				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Chorale Preludes, BWV 714-765 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>

</th>
<td>56 pieces
<ol><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Ach_Gott_und_Herr,_BWV_714_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Ach Gott und Herr, BWV 714 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Ach Gott und Herr, BWV 714</a></i> ("per canonem")
</li><li> Allein Gott in der Höh sei Eh, BWV 715r (VIII)
</li><li> Fuga super 'Allein Gott in der Höh sei Ehr', BWV 716
</li><li> Allein Gott in der Höh sei Ehr, BWV 717 (IX)
</li><li> Fantasia sopra Christ lag in Todesbanden, BWV 718 (II)
</li><li> Der Tag, der ist so freudenreich, BWV 719 (II) - also attributed to <a href="/wiki/Category:Pachelbel,_Johann" title="Category:Pachelbel, Johann">Johann Pachelbel</a>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Ein_feste_Burg_ist_unser_Gott,_BWV_720_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott, BWV 720 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott, BWV 720</a></i> - possibly by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Michael" title="Category:Bach, Johann Michael">Johann Michael Bach</a>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Erbarm_dich_mein,_o_Herre_Gott,_BWV_721_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Erbarm dich mein, o Herre Gott, BWV 721 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Erbarm dich mein, o Herre Gott, BWV 721</a></i>
</li><li> Gelobet seist du, Jesu Christ, BWV 722 (III)
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Gelobet_seist_du,_Jesu_Christ,_BWV_723_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Gelobet seist du, Jesu Christ, BWV 723 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Gelobet seist du, Jesu Christ, BWV 723</a></i> - possibly by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Michael" title="Category:Bach, Johann Michael">Johann Michael Bach</a>
</li><li> Gott, durch deine Güte, BWV 724 ("Gottes Sohn ist kommen")
</li><li> Herr Gott, dich loben wir, BWV 725
</li><li> Herr Jesu Christ, dich zu unswend, BWV 726 (III)
</li><li> Herzlich tut mich verlangen, BWV 727
</li><li> Jesus, meine Zuversicht, BWV 728
</li><li> In dulci jubilo, BWV 729 (II)
</li><li> In dulci jubilo, BWV 729a (III)
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Liebster_Jesu,_wir_sind_hier,_BWV_730_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Liebster Jesu, wir sind hier, BWV 730 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Liebster Jesu, wir sind hier, BWV 730</a></i> (IV)
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Liebster_Jesu,_wir_sind_hier,_BWV_731_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Liebster Jesu, wir sind hier, BWV 731 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Liebster Jesu, wir sind hier, BWV 731</a></i> (V)
</li><li> Lobt Gott, ihr Christen,allzugleich (II), BWV 732
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Fuga_sopra_il_Magnificat,_BWV_733_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fuga sopra il Magnificat, BWV 733 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fuga sopra il Magnificat, BWV 733</a></i>

</dd></dl>
</li><li> Nun freut euch, lieben Christen gmein (I), BWV 734
</li><li> Nun freut euch, lieben Christen gmein (II), BWV 734a
</li><li> Fantasia super Valet will ich dir geben, BWV 735
</li><li> Valet will ich dir geben, BWV 736
</li><li> Vater unser im Himmelreich (IV), BWV 737
</li><li> Vom Himmel hoch, da komm ich her (IV), BWV 738
</li><li> Vom Himmel hoch, da komm ich her (V), BWV 738a
</li><li> Wie schön leuchtet der Morgenstern (I), BWV 739
</li><li> Wir glauben all' an einen Gott (IV), BWV 740 - likely spurious
<dl><dd>probably <i><a href="/wiki/Wir_glauben_all%27_an_einen_Gott_(Krebs,_Johann_Ludwig)" title="Wir glauben all' an einen Gott (Krebs, Johann Ludwig)">Wir glauben all' an einen Gott</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Krebs,_Johann_Ludwig" title="Category:Krebs, Johann Ludwig">Johann Ludwig Krebs</a> (Krebs‑WV 554c)
</dd></dl>
</li><li> Ach Gott vom Himmel sieh darein, BWV 741
</li><li> Ach Herr, mich armen Sünder, BWV 742
</li><li> Ach, was ist doch unser Leben, BWV 743
</li><li> Auf meinen lieben Gott, BWV 744 - likely spurious

</li><li> <b>BWV 573</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fantasia_in_C_major,_BWV_573_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fantasia in C major, BWV 573 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fantasia in C major</a></i> (fragment)
</li><li> <b>BWV 574</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fuge_%C3%BCber_ein_Thema_von_Giovanni_Legrenzi,_BWV_574_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fuge über ein Thema von Giovanni Legrenzi, BWV 574 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Fuge über ein Thema von Giovanni Legrenzi</a></i> (Fugue on a Theme by Giovanni Legrenzi)
</li><li> <b>BWV 575</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_C_minor,_BWV_575_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in C minor, BWV 575 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fugue in C minor</a></i>
</li><li> <b>BWV 576</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_G_major,_BWV_576_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in G major, BWV 576 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fugue in G major</a></i> (spurious)
</li><li> <b>BWV 577</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_G_major,_BWV_577_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in G major, BWV 577 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fugue in G major</a></i>
</li><li> <b>BWV 578</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_G_minor,_BWV_578_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in G minor, BWV 578 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fugue in G minor</a></i> ("Little")
</li><li> <b>BWV 579</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fuge_%C3%BCber_ein_Thema_von_Corelli,_BWV_579_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fuge über ein Thema von Corelli, BWV 579 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Fuge über ein Thema von Corelli</a></i> (Fugue on a Theme by Corelli)
</li><li> <b>BWV 580</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_D_major,_BWV_580_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in D major, BWV 580 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Fugue in D major</a></i> (spurious)
</li><li> <b>BWV 581</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_G_major,_BWV_581_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in G major, BWV 581 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Fugue in G major</a></i> (spurious)
</li><li> <b>BWV 582</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Passacaglia_in_C_minor,_BWV_582_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Passacaglia in C minor, BWV 582 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Passacaglia in C minor</a></i>
</li><li> <b>BWV Anh.90</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Fugue_in_C_major,_BWV_Anh.90_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Fugue in C major, BWV Anh.90 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Fugue in C major</a></i> (doubtful)
</li></ul>

</li><li><b>BWV 769</b> — <a href="/wiki/Vom_himmel_hoch,_da_komm_ich_her,_BWV_769_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Vom himmel hoch, da komm ich her, BWV 769 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)" class="mw-redirect">Canonic variations on "Vom Himmel hoch, da komm' ich her"</a>

</li><li><b>BWV 771</b> — <a href="/wiki/Allein_Gott_in_der_H%C3%B6h_sei_Ehr_(Vetter,_Nicolaus)" title="Allein Gott in der Höh sei Ehr (Vetter, Nicolaus)">Chorale variations "Allein Gott in der Höh' sei Ehr'" (spurious; now attributed to Nicolaus Vetter)</a>
